                                        SELECT id_category, fatherCategory, url
                                        FROM categories
                                        WHERE url = 'tecnologia'
                                        UNION
                                        SELECT c.id_category, c.fatherCategory, c.url
                                        FROM categories c
                                        JOIN category_path cp ON c.id_category = cp.fatherCategory
                                    )
                                    SELECT url
                                    FROM category_path
                                    ORDER BY id_category

                                            SELECT id_category, fatherCategory, url
                                            FROM categories
                                            WHERE url = 'tecnologia'

                                            SELECT c.id_category, c.fatherCategory, c.url
                                            FROM categories c
                                            JOIN category_path cp ON c.id_category = cp.fatherCategory
                                        )
                                        SELECT url

                                        ORDER BY id_category

[2023/12/19 11:39:02] SQL Query:   WITH RECURSIVE category_path AS (
                                        SELECT id_category, fatherCategory, url
                                        FROM categories
                                        WHERE url = 'tecnologia'
                                        UNION
                                        SELECT c.id_category, c.fatherCategory, c.url
                                        FROM categories c
                                        JOIN category_path cp ON c.id_category = cp.fatherCategory
                                    )
                                    SELECT url
                                    FROM category_path
                                    ORDER BY id_category
